Source Code

These source-code files were from the printout at the MIT Museum, with many thanks to Deborah Douglas, the Museum's Curator of Science and Technology, for releasing it to us. The printout was digitally photographed by Paul Fjeld. A team of volunteers transcribed the source code manually from these images or, where appropriate, modified already-transcribed but similar source Luminary 131 (Apollo 13) source code to agree with the images from the printout. Note that the page images presented online are of reduced quality, and that higher-quality images are available. Report any conversion errors or legibility problems in page images to info@sandroid.org. Notations on the program listing read, in part:

	GAP:  ASSEMBLE REVISION 001 OF AGC PROGRAM LMY99 BY NASA 2021112-061
	20'35 OCT. 28,1968
Note that the date is the date of the printout, not the date of the program revision.

Page 390 

016532,000043:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME - KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY PROGRAM
016533,000044:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO - 4            DATE - 27 APRIL 1967            ASSEMBLY - PINDANCE REV 18
016534,000045:                                                                                                  #  MOD BY - FILENE
016535,000046:                                                                                                  #  LOG SECTION - PINBALL GAME BUTTONS AND LIGHTS
016536,000047: 
016537,000048:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION-
016538,000049: 
016539,000050:                                                                                                  #  THE KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY SYSTEM PROGRAM OPERATES UNDER EXECUTIVE
016540,000051:                                                                                                  #  CONTROL AND PROCESSES INFORMATION EXCHANGED BETWEEN THE AGC AND THE
016541,000052:                                                                                                  #  COMPUTER OPERATOR.  THE INPUTS TO THE PROGRAM ARE FROM THE KEYBOARD,
016542,000053:                                                                                                  #  FROM INTERNAL PROGRAMS, AND FROM THE UPLINK.
016543,000054: 
016544,000055:                                                                                                  #  THE LANGUAGE OF COMMUNICATION WITH THE PROGRAM IS A PAIR OF WORDS
016545,000056:                                                                                                  #  KNOWN AS VERB AND NOUN.  EACH OF THESE IS REPRESENTED BY A 2 CHARACTER
016546,000057:                                                                                                  #  DECIMAL NUMBER.  THE VERB CODE INDICATES WHAT ACTION IS TO BE TAKEN, THE
016547,000058:                                                                                                  #  NOUN CODE INDICATES TO WHAT THIS ACTION IS APPLIED.  NOUNS USUALLY
016548,000059:                                                                                                  #  REFER TO A GROUP OF ERASABLE REGISTERS.
016549,000060: 
016550,000061:                                                                                                  #  VERBS ARE GROUPED INTO DISPLAYS, LOADS, MONITORS (DISPLAYS THAT ARE
016551,000062:                                                                                                  #  UPDATED ONCE PER SECOND), SPECIAL FUNCTIONS, AND EXTENDED VERBS (THESE
016552,000063:                                                                                                  #  ARE OUTSIDE OF THE DOMAIN OF PINBALL AND CAN BE FOUND UNDER LOG SECTION
016553,000064:                                                                                                  #  :EXTENDED VERBS:).
016554,000065: 
016555,000066:                                                                                                  #  A LIST OF VERBS AND NOUNS IS GIVEN IN LOG SECTION :ASSEMBLY AND 
016556,000067:                                                                                                  #  OPERATION INFORMATION:.
016557,000068:

Ramón Alonso, one of the original AGC developers, provides a little more insight: Apparently, nobody had yet arrived at any kind of software requirements for the AGC's user interface when the desire arose within the Instrumentation Laboratory to set up a demo guidance-computer unit with which to impress visitors to the lab. Of course, this demo would have to do something, if it was going to be at all impressive, and to do something it would need some software. In short order, some of the coders threw together a demo program, inventing and using the verb/noun user-interface concept (in the whimsical fashion seen in much of this code), but without any idea that the verb/noun concept would somehow survive into the flight software. As time passed, and more and more people became familiar with the demo, nobody got around to inventing an improvement for the user interface, so the coders simply built it into the flight software without any specific requirements to do so.

However, that does not mean that the verb/noun interface was universally beloved. Ramón says that many objections were received from naysayers, such as "it's not scientific", "it's not dignified", or even "astronauts won't understand it". Even though the coders of the demo hadn't seriously intended the verb/noun interface to be used in any permanent way, it became a kind of devilish game to counter these objections with (perhaps) sophistic arguments as to why the interface was really a good one. In the end, the coders won. I don't know whether they were elated or dismayed by this victory.

The astronauts, of course, could understand the interface, but they did not like it. Most of them really wanted an interface much more like that they had used in aircraft: i.e., lots of dials and switches. Dave Scott is the the only astronaut I'm aware of who had kind words for it (or for the AGC in general), though we are told that Jim McDivitt wasn't necessary completely hostile to it.

—Ron Burkey, 07/2009

016592,000103: 
016593,000104:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCES -
016594,000105: 
016595,000106:                                                                                                  #  KEYBOARD:
016596,000107:                                                                                                  #  EACH DEPRESSION OF A KEYBOARD BUTTON ACTIVATES INTERRUPT KEYRUPT1
016597,000108:                                                                                                  #  AND PLACES THE 5 BIT KEY CODE INTO CHANNEL 15.  KEYRUPT1 PLACES THE KEY
016598,000109:                                                                                                  #  CODE INTO MPAC, ENTERS AN EXECUTIVE REQUEST FOR THE KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY
016599,000110:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM (AT :CHARIN:), AND EXECUTES A RESUME.
016600,000111: 
016601,000112:                                                                                                  #  UPLINK:
016602,000113:                                                                                                  #  EACH WORD RECEIVED BY THE UPLINK ACTIVATES INTERRUPT UPRUPT WHICH
016603,000114:                                                                                                  #  PLACES THE 5 BIT KEY CODE INTO MPAC, ENTERS AN EXECUTIVE REQUEST FOR THE
016604,000115:                                                                                                  #  KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY PROGRAM (AT :CHARIN:) AND EXECUTES A RESUME.
016605,000116: 
016606,000117:                                                                                                  #  INTERNAL PROGRAMS:
016607,000118:                                                                                                  #  INTERNAL PROGRAMS CALL PINBALL AT :NVSUB: WITH THE DESIRED VERB/NOUN
016608,000119:                                                                                                  #  CODE IN A (LOW 7 BITS FOR NOUN, NEXT 7 BITS FOR VERB).  DETAILS
016609,000120:                                                                                                  #  DESCRIBED ON REMARKS CARDS JUST BEFORE :NVSUB: AND :NVSBWAIT: (SEE
016610,000121:                                                                                                  #  SYMBOL TABLE FOR PAGE NUMBERS).
016611,000122: 
016612,000123:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES -
016613,000124: 
016614,000125:                                                                                                  #        IF PINBALL WAS CALLED BY EXTERNAL ACTION, THERE ARE FOUR EXITS:
016615,000126:                                                                                                  #                1)      ALL BUT (2), (3), AND (4) EXIT DIRECTLY TO ENDOFJOB.
016616,000127:                                                                                                  #                2)      EXTENDED VERBS GO TO THE EXTENDED VERB FAN AS PART OF THE

Page 391 

016618,000129:                                                                                                  #                        PINBALL EXECUTIVE JOB WITH PRIORITY 30000.  IT IS THE 
016619,000130:                                                                                                  #                        RESPONSIBILITY OF THE EXTENDED VERB CALLED TO EVENTUALLY
016620,000131:                                                                                                  #                        CHANGE PRIORITY (IF NECESSARY) AND DO AN ENDOFJOB.
016621,000132:                                                                                                  #                        ALSO PINBALL IS A NOVAC JOB.  EBANK SET FOR COMMON.
016622,000133:                                                                                                  #                3)      VERB 37.  CHANGE OF PROGRAM (MAJOR MODE) CALLS :V37: IN THE
016623,000134:                                                                                                  #                        SERVICE ROUTINES AS PART OF THE PINBALL EXEC JOB WITH PRIO
016624,000135:                                                                                                  #                        30000.  THE NEW PROGRAM CODE (MAJOR MODE) IS LEFT IN A.
016625,000136:                                                                                                  #                4)      KEY RELEASE BUTTON CALLS :PINBRNCH: IN THE DISPLAY INTERFACE
016626,000137:                                                                                                  #                        ROUTINES AS PART OF THE PINBALL EXEC JOB WITH PRIO 30000 IF 
016627,000138:                                                                                                  #                        THE KEY RELEASE LIGHT IS OFF AND :CADRSTOR: IS NOT +0.
016628,000139: 
016629,000140:                                                                                                  #  IF PINBALL WAS CALLED BY INTERNAL PROGRAMS, EXIT FROM PINBALL IS BACK
016630,000141:                                                                                                  #  TO CALLING ROUTINE.  DETAILS DESCRIBED IN REMARKS CARDS JUST BEFORE
016631,000142:                                                                                                  #  :NVSUB: AND :NVSBWAIT: (SEE SYMBOL TABLE FOR PAGE NUMBERS).
016632,000143: 
016633,000144:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES -
016634,000145: 
016635,000146:                                                                                                  #        EXTERNAL INITIATION:
016636,000147:                                                                                                  #        IF SOME IMPROPER SEQUENCE OF KEY CODES IS DETECTED, THE OPERATOR
016637,000148:                                                                                                  #        ERROR LIGHT IS TURNED ON AND EXIT IS TO :ENDOFJOB:.
016638,000149: 
016639,000150:                                                                                                  #        INTERNAL PROGRAM INITIATION:
016640,000151:                                                                                                  #        IF AN ILLEGAL V/N COMBINATION IS ATTEMPTED, AN ABORT IS CAUSED
016641,000152:                                                                                                  #        (WITH OCTAL 01501).
016642,000153:                                                                                                  #        IF A SECOND ATTEMPT IS MADE TO GO TO SLEEP IN PINBALL, AN ABORT IS
016643,000154:                                                                                                  #        CAUSED (WITH OCTAL 01206). THERE ARE TWO WAYS TO GO TO SLEEP IN PINBALL:
016644,000155:                                                                                                  #                1) ENDIDLE OR DATAWAIT.
016645,000156:                                                                                                  #                2) NVSBWAIT, PRENVBSY, OR NVSUBUSY.
016646,000157: 
016647,000158:                                                                                                  #  CONDITIONS LEADING TO THE ABOVE ARE DESCRIBED IN FORTHCOMING MIT/IL
016648,000159:                                                                                                  #  E-REPORT DESCRIBING KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY OPERATION FOR 278.
016649,000160: 
016650,000161:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT -
016651,000162: 
016652,000163:                                                                                                  #  INFORMATION TO BE SENT TO THE DISPLAY PANEL IS LEFT IN THE :DSPTAB:
016653,000164:                                                                                                  #  BUFFERS REGISTERS (UNDER EXEC CONTROL). :DSPOUT: (A PART OF T4RUPT)
016654,000165:                                                                                                  #  HANDLES THE PLACING OF THE :DSPTAB: INFORMATION INTO OUTPUT CHANNEL 10
016655,000166:                                                                                                  #  IN INTERRUPT.
016656,000167: 
016657,000168:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION -
016658,000169: 
016659,000170:                                                                                                  #  FRESH START AND RESTART INITIALIZE THE NECESSARY E REGISTERS FOR
016660,000171:                                                                                                  #  PINBALL IN :STARTSUB:.  REGISTERS ARE:  DSPTAB BUFFER, CADRSTOR,
016661,000172:                                                                                                  #  REQRET, CLPASS, DSPLOCK, MONSAVE, MONSAVE1, VERBREG, NOUNREG, DSPLIST,
016662,000173:                                                                                                  #  DSPCOUNT, NOUT.
016663,000174: 
016664,000175:                                                                                                  #  A COMPLETE LIST OF ALL THE ERASABLES (BOTH RESERVED AND TEMPORARIES) FOR

Page 392 

016666,000177:                                                                                                  #  PINBALL IS GIVEN BELOW.
016667,000178: 
016668,000179:                                                                                                  #  THE FOLLOWING ARE OF GENERAL INTEREST -
016669,000180: 
016670,000181:                                                                                                  #  REMARKS CARDS PRECEDE THE REFERENCED SYMBOL DEFINITION.  SEE SYMBOL
016671,000182:                                                                                                  #  TABLE TO FIND APPROPRIATE PAGE NUMBERS.
016672,000183: 
016673,000184:                                                                                                  #        NVSUB           CALLING POINT FOR INTERNAL USE OF PINBALL.
016674,000185:                                                                                                  #                        OF RELATED INTEREST     NVSBWAIT
016675,000186:                                                                                                  #                                                NVSUBUSY
016676,000187:                                                                                                  #                                                PRENVBSY
016677,000188: 
016678,000189:                                                                                                  #        ENDIDLE         ROUTINE FOR INTERNAL PROGRAMS WISHING TO GO TO SLEEP WHILE
016679,000190:                                                                                                  #                        AWAITING OPERATORS RESPONSE.
016680,000191: 
016681,000192:                                                                                                  #        DSPMM           ROUTINE BY WHICH AN INTERNAL PROGRAM MAY DISPLAY A DECIMAL
016682,000193:                                                                                                  #                        PROGRAM CODE (MAJOR MODE) IN THE PROGRAM (MAJOR MODE) LIGHTS.
016683,000194:                                                                                                  #                        (DSPMM DOES NOT DISPLAY DIRECTLY BUT ENTERS EXEC REQUEST
016684,000195:                                                                                                  #                        FOR DSPMMJB WITH PRIO 30000 AND RETURNS TO CALLER.)
016685,000196: 
016686,000197:                                                                                                  #        BLANKSUB        ROUTINE BY WHICH AN INTERNAL PROGRAM MAY BLANK ANY
016687,000198:                                                                                                  #                        COMBINATION OF THE DISPLAY REGISTERS R1, R2, R3.
016688,000199: 
016689,000200:                                                                                                  #        JAMTERM         ROUTINES BY WHICH AN INTERNAL PROGRAM MAY PERFORM THE
016690,000201:                                                                                                  #        JAMPROC         TERMINATE (V 34) OR PROCEED (V 33) FUNCTION.
016691,000202: 
016692,000203:                                                                                                  #        MONITOR         VERBS FOR PERIODIC (1 PER SEC) DISPLAY.
016693,000204: 
016694,000205:                                                                                                  #        PLEASE PERFORM, PLEASE MARK SITUATIONS
016695,000206:                                                                                                  #                REMARKS DESCRIBING HOW AN INTERNAL ROUTINE SHOULD HANDLE
016696,000207:                                                                                                  #                THESE SITUATIONS CAN BE FOUND JUST BEFORE :NVSUB: (SEE
016697,000208:                                                                                                  #                SYMBOL TABLE FOR PAGE NUMBER).
016698,000209: 
016699,000210:                                                                                                  #        THE NOUN TABLE FORMAT IS DESCRIBED ON A PAGE OF REMARKS CARDS JUST
016700,000211:                                                                                                  #        BEFORE :DSPABC: (SEE SYMBOL TABLE FOR PAGE NUMBER).
016701,000212: 
016702,000213:                                                                                                  #        THE NOUN TABLES THEMSELVES ARE FOUND IN LOG SECTION :PINBALL NOUN
016703,000214:                                                                                                  #        TABLES:.
016704,000215: 
016705,000216:                                                                                                  #  FOR FURTHER DETAILS ABOUT OPERATION OF THE KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY SYSTEM
016706,000217:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM, SEE THE MISSION PLAN AND/OR MIT/IL E-2129
016707,000218:                                                                                                  #  DESCRIBING KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY OPERATION FOR 278.
016708,000219:

The document described above, "Keyboard and Display Program Operation" by Alan I. Green and Robert J. Filene is available online at the Virtual AGC website. —Ron Burkey, 07/2009

016726,000237:                                                                                                  #  THE FOLLOWING ASSIGNMENTS FOR PINBALL ARE MADE ELSEWHERE
016727,000238: 
016728,000239:                                                                                                  #  RESERVED FOR PINBALL EXECUTIVE ACTION
016729,000240: 
016730,000241:                                                                                                  #  DSPCOUNT      ERASE                   DISPLAY POSITION INDICATOR
016731,000242:                                                                                                  #  DECBRNCH      ERASE                   +DEC, -DEC, OCT INDICATOR
016732,000243:                                                                                                  #  VERBREG       ERASE                   VERB CODE
016733,000244:                                                                                                  #  NOUNREG       ERASE                   NOUN CODE
016734,000245:                                                                                                  #  XREG          ERASE                   R1 INPUT BUFFER
016735,000246:                                                                                                  #  YREG          ERASE                   R2 INPUT BUFFER
016736,000247:                                                                                                  #  ZREG          ERASE                   R3 INPUT BUFFER
016737,000248:                                                                                                  #  XREGLP        ERASE                   LO PART OF XREG (FOR DEC CONV ONLY)
016738,000249:                                                                                                  #  YREGLP        ERASE                   LO PART OF YREG (FOR DEC CONV ONLY)
016739,000250:                                                                                                  #  HITEMOUT      =       YREGLP          TEMP FOR DISPLAY OF HRS, MIN, SEC
016740,000251:                                                                                                  #                                                MUST = LOTEMOUT-1.
016741,000252:                                                                                                  #  ZREGLP        ERASE                   LO PART OF ZREG (FOR DEC CONV ONLY)
016742,000253:                                                                                                  #  LOTEMOUT      =       ZREGLP          TEMP FOR DISPLAY OF HRS, MIN, SEC
016743,000254:                                                                                                  #                                                MUST = HITEMOUT+1.
016744,000255:                                                                                                  #  MODREG        ERASE                   MODE CODE
016745,000256:                                                                                                  #  DSPLOCK       ERASE                   KEYBOARD/SUBROUTINE CALL INTERLOCK
016746,000257:                                                                                                  #  REQRET        ERASE                   RETURN REGISTER FOR LOAD
016747,000258:                                                                                                  #  LOADSTAT      ERASE                   STATUS INDICATOR FOR LOADTST
016748,000259:                                                                                                  #  CLPASS        ERASE                   PASS INDICATOR CLEAR
016749,000260:                                                                                                  #  NOUT          ERASE                   ACTIVITY COUNTER FOR DSPTAB
016750,000261:                                                                                                  #  NOUNCADR      ERASE                   MACHINE CADR FOR NOUN
016751,000262:                                                                                                  #  MONSAVE       ERASE                   N/V CODE FOR MONITOR. (= MONSAVE1-1)
016752,000263:                                                                                                  #  MONSAVE1      ERASE                   NOUNCADR FOR MONITOR (MATBS) = MONSAVE+1
016753,000264:                                                                                                  #  MONSAVE2      ERASE                   NVMONOPT OPTIONS
016754,000265:                                                                                                  #  DSPTAB        ERASE           +13D    0-10, DISPLAY PANEL BUFFER.11-13, C RELAYS
016755,000266:                                                                                                  #  CADRSTOR      ERASE                   ENDIDLE STORAGE
016756,000267:                                                                                                  #  NVQTEM        ERASE                   NVSUB STORAGE FOR CALLING ADDRESS
016757,000268:                                                                                                  #                                        MUST = NVBNKTEM-1
016758,000269:                                                                                                  #  NVBNKTEM      ERASE                   NVSUB STORAGE FOR CALLING BANK
016759,000270:                                                                                                  #                                        MUST = NVQTEM+1
016760,000271:                                                                                                  #  VERBSAVE      ERASE                   NEEDED FOR RECYCLE
016761,000272:                                                                                                  #  DSPLIST       ERASE                   WAITING REG FOR DSP SYST INTERNAL USE
016762,000273:                                                                                                  #  EXTVBACT      REASE                   EXTENDED VERB ACTIVITY INTERLOCK
016763,000274:                                                                                                  #  DSPTEM1       ERASE           +2      BUFFER STORAGE AREA 1 (MOSTLY FOR TIME)
016764,000275:                                                                                                  #  DSPTEM2       ERASE           +2      BUFFER STORAGE AREA 2 (MOSTLY FOR DEG)
016765,000276: 
016766,000277:                                                                                                  #  END OF ERASABLES RESERVED FOR PINBALL EXECUTIVE ACTION
016767,000278:

016790,000301: 
016791,000302:                                                                                                  #  SGNOFF        =       VBUF    +1      TEMP FOR +,- ON
016792,000303:                                                                                                  #  NVTEMP        =       VBUF    +1      TEMP FOR NVSUB
016793,000304:                                                                                                  #  SFTEMP1       =       VBUF    +1      STORAGE FOR SF CONST HI PART (=SFTEMP2-1)
016794,000305:                                                                                                  #  HITEMIN       =       VBUF    +1      TEMP FOR LOAD OF HRS, MIN, SEC
016795,000306:                                                                                                  #                                                MUST = LOTEMIN-1.
016796,000307:                                                                                                  #  CODE          =       VBUF    +2      FOR DSPIN
016797,000308:                                                                                                  #  SFTEMP2       =       VBUF    +2      STORAGE FOR SF CONST LO PART (=SFTEMP1+1)
016798,000309:                                                                                                  #  LOTEMIN       =       VBUF    +2      TEMP FOR LOAD OF HRS, MIN, SEC
016799,000310:                                                                                                  #                                                MUST = HITEMIN+1.
016800,000311:                                                                                                  #  MIXTEMP       =       VBUF    +3      FOR MIXNOUN DATA
016801,000312:                                                                                                  #  SIGNRET       =       VBUF    +3      RETURN FOR +,- ON

2003 RSB — The PROCEED key has no keycode; it is read by an alternate mechanism. 

016886,000397: 
016887,000398:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT FORMAT FOR DISPLAY PANEL.  SET OUT0 TO AAAABCCCCCDDDDD.
016888,000399:                                                                                                  #  A-S   SELECT A RELAYWORD. THIS DETERMINES WHICH PAIR OF CHARACTERS ARE
016889,000400:                                                                                                  #        ENERGIZED.
016890,000401:                                                                                                  #  B     FOR SPECIAL RELAYS SUCH AS SIGNS ETC.
016891,000402:                                                                                                  #  C-S   5 BIT RELAY CODE FOR LEFT CHAR OF PAIR SELECTED BY RELAYWORD
016892,000403:                                                                                                  #  D-S   5 BIT RELAY CODE FOR RIGHT CHAR OF PAIR SELECTED BY RELAYWORD.
016893,000404: 
016894,000405:                                                                                                  #  THE PANEL APPEARS AS FOLLOWS,
016895,000406:                                                                                                  #  MD1   MD2                             (MAJOR MODE)
016896,000407:                                                                                                  #  VD1   VD2 (VERB)      ND1     ND2     (NOUN)
016897,000408:                                                                                                  #  R1D1  R1D2    R1D3    R1D4    R1D5    (R1)
016898,000409:                                                                                                  #  R2D1  R2D2    R2D3    R2D4    R2D5    (R2)
016899,000410:                                                                                                  #  R3D1  R3D2    R3D3    R3D4    R3D5    (R3)
016900,000411: 
016901,000412:                                                                                                  #  EACH OF THESE IS GIVEN A DSPCOUNT NUMBER FOR USE WITHIN COMPUTATION ONLY
016902,000413: 
016903,000414:                                                                                                  #  MD1   25              R2D1    11              ALL ARE OCTAL
016904,000415:                                                                                                  #  MD2   24              R2D2    10
016905,000416:                                                                                                  #  VD1   23              R2D3     7
016906,000417:                                                                                                  #  VD2   22              R2D4     6
016907,000418:                                                                                                  #  ND1   21              R2D5     5
016908,000419:                                                                                                  #  ND2   20              R3D1     4
016909,000420:                                                                                                  #  R1D1  16              R3D2     3
016910,000421:                                                                                                  #  R1D2  15              R3D3     2
016911,000422:                                                                                                  #  R1D3  14              R3D4     1
016912,000423:                                                                                                  #  R1D4  13              R3D5     0
016913,000424:                                                                                                  #  R1D5  12
016914,000425: 
016915,000426:                                                                                                  #  THERE IS AN 11 REGISTER TABLE (DSPTAB) FOR THE DISPLAY PANEL.
016916,000427: 
016917,000428:                                                                                                  #  DSPTAB                RELAYWD         BIT11           BITS 10-6       BITS 5-1
016918,000429:                                                                                                  #  RELADD
016919,000430:                                                                                                  #  10            1011                            MD1 (25)        MD2 (24)
016920,000431:                                                                                                  #  9             1010                            VD1 (23)        VD2 (22)
016921,000432:                                                                                                  #  8             1001                            ND1 (21)        ND2 (20)
016922,000433:                                                                                                  #  7             1000                                            R1D1 (16)

Page 397 

016924,000435:                                                                                                  #  6             0111            +R1             R1D2 (15)       R1D3 (14)
016925,000436:                                                                                                  #  5             0110            -R1             R1D4 (13)       R1D5 (12)
016926,000437:                                                                                                  #  4             0101            +R2             R2D1 (11)       R2D2 (10)
016927,000438:                                                                                                  #  3             0100            -R2             R2D3 (7)        R2D4 (6)
016928,000439:                                                                                                  #  2             0011                            R2D5 (5)        R3D1 (4)
016929,000440:                                                                                                  #  1             0010            +R3             R3D2 (3)        R3D3 (2)
016930,000441:                                                                                                  #  0             0001            -R3             R3D4 (1)        R3D5 (0)
016931,000442:                                                                                                  #                0000        NO RELAYWORD
016932,000443: 
016933,000444:                                                                                                  #  THE 5 BIT OUTPUT RELAY CODES ARE:
016934,000445: 
016935,000446:                                                                                                  #  BLANK 00000
016936,000447:                                                                                                  #  0     10101
016937,000448:                                                                                                  #  1     00011
016938,000449:                                                                                                  #  2     11001
016939,000450:                                                                                                  #  3     11011
016940,000451:                                                                                                  #  4     01111
016941,000452:                                                                                                  #  5     11110
016942,000453:                                                                                                  #  6     11100
016943,000454:                                                                                                  #  7     10011
016944,000455:                                                                                                  #  8     11101
016945,000456:                                                                                                  #  9     11111
016946,000457: 
016947,000458:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT BITS USED BY PINBALL:
016948,000459: 
016949,000460:                                                                                                  #        KEY RELEASE LIGHT       -       BIT 5 OF CHANNEL 11
016950,000461:                                                                                                  #        VERB/NOUN FLASH         -       BIT 6 OF CHANNEL 11
016951,000462:                                                                                                  #        OPERATOR ERROR LIGHT    -       BIT 7 OF CHANNEL 11

017641,001152: 41,2352           61420                           CADR     DSPALARM                              
017642,001153:

Page 413 

017644,001155:                                                                                                  #  NOUN TABLES
017645,001156: 
017646,001157:                                                                                                  #  NOUN CODE L/40, NORMAL NOUN CASE.  NOUN CODE G/E 40, MIXED NOUN CASE.
017647,001158:                                                                                                  #  FOR NORMAL CASE, NNADTAB CONTAINS ONE       ECADR     FOR EACH NOUN.
017648,001159:                                                                                                  #  +0 INDICATES NOUN NOT USED.   - ENTRY INDICATES MACHINE CADR (E OR F) TO
017649,001160:                                                                                                  #  BE SPECIFIED. -1 INDICATES CHANNEL TO BE SPECIFIED.  -0 INDICATES AUGMENT
017650,001161:                                                                                                  #  OF LAST MACHINE CADR SUPPLIED.
017651,001162: 
017652,001163:                                                                                                  #  FOR MIXED CASE, NNADTAB CONTAINS ONE INDIRECT ADDRESS (IDADDREL) IN LOW
017653,001164:                                                                                                  #  10 BITS, AND THE COMPONENT CODE NUMBER IN THE HIGH 5 BITS.
017654,001165: 
017655,001166:                                                                                                  #  NNTYPTAB IS A PACKED TABLE OF THE FORM MMMMMNNNNNPPPPP.
017656,001167: 
017657,001168:                                                                                                  #  FOR THE NORMAL CASE,  M-S ARE THE COMPONENT CODE NUMBER.
017658,001169:                                                                                                  #                        N-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE CODE NUMBER.
017659,001170:                                                                                                  #                        P-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT CODE NUMBER.
017660,001171: 
017661,001172:                                                                                                  #  MIXED CASE,           M-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT3 CODE NUMBER    3 COMPONENT CASE
017662,001173:                                                                                                  #                        N-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT2 CODE NUMBER
017663,001174:                                                                                                  #                        P-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT1 CODE NUMBER
017664,001175:                                                                                                  #                        N-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT2 CODE NUMBER    2 COMPONENT CASE
017665,001176:                                                                                                  #                        P-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT1 CODE NUMBER
017666,001177:                                                                                                  #                        P-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT1 CODE NUMBER    1 COMPONENT CASE
017667,001178: 
017668,001179:                                                                                                  #  THERE IS ALSO AN INDIRECT ADDRESS TABLE (IDADDTAB) FOR MIXED CASE ONLY.
017669,001180:                                                                                                  #  EACH ENTRY CONTAINS ONE ECADR.    IDADDREL IS THE RELATIVE ADDRESS OF
017670,001181:                                                                                                  #  THE FIRST OF THESE ENTRIES.
017671,001182:                                                                                                  #  THERE IS ONE ENTRY IN THIS TABLE FOR EACH COMPONENT OF A MIXED NOUN
017672,001183:                                                                                                  #  THEY ARE LISTED IN ORDER OF ASCENDING K.
017673,001184: 
017674,001185:                                                                                                  #  THERE IS ALSO A SCALE FACTOR ROUTINE NUMBER TABLE (RUTMXTAB) FOR MIXED
017675,001186:                                                                                                  #  CASE ONLY.  THERE IS ONE ENTRY PER MIXED NOUN.  THE FORM IS,
017676,001187: 
017677,001188:                                                                                                  #        QQQQQRRRRRSSSSS
017678,001189: 
017679,001190:                                                                                                  #  Q-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 3 CODE NUMBER          3 COMPONENT CASE
017680,001191:                                                                                                  #  R-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 2 CODE NUMBER
017681,001192:                                                                                                  #  S-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 1 CODE NUMBER
017682,001193:                                                                                                  #  R-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 2 CODE NUMBER          2 COMPONENT CASE
017683,001194:                                                                                                  #  S-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 1 CODE NUMBER
017684,001195: 
017685,001196:                                                                                                  #  IN OCTAL DISPLAY AND LOAD (OCT OR DEC) VERBS, EXCLUDE USE OF VERBS WHOSE
017686,001197:                                                                                                  #  COMPONENT NUMBER IS GREATER THAN THE NUMBER OF COMPONENTS IN NOUN.
017687,001198:                                                                                                  #  (ALL MACHINE ADDRESS TO BE SPECIFIED NOUNS ARE 3 COMPONENT.)
017688,001199: 
017689,001200:                                                                                                  #  IN MULTI-COMPONENT LOAD VERBS, NO MIXING OF OCTAL AND DECIMAL DATA
017690,001201:                                                                                                  #  COMPONENT WORDS IS ALLOWED. ALARM IF VIOLATION.
017691,001202: 
017692,001203:                                                                                                  #  IN DECIMAL LOADS OF DATA, 5 NUMERICAL CHARACTERS MUST BE KEYED IN
017693,001204:                                                                                                  #  BEFORE EACH ENTER. IF NOT, ALARM.

018000,001511: 
018001,001512:                                                                                                  #  THE FOLLOWING ROUTINE DISPLAYS TWO CONTIGUOUS SP POSITIVE INTEGERS
018002,001513:                                                                                                  #  AS TWO POSITIVE DECIMAL INTEGERS IN RXD1-RXD2 AND RXD4-RXD5 (RXD3 IS

018212,001723:                                                                                                  #  OF THE REGISTER NOUNADD IS POINTING TO.  IF USED WITH NOUNS WHICH ARE
018213,001724:                                                                                                  #  INHERENTLY NOT DP SUCH AS THE CDU COUNTERS THE DISPLAY WILL BE GARBAGE.

018807,002318:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR ALLOWS OTHER KEYBOARD ACTIVITY. IT IS ENDED BY VERB TERMINATE,
018808,002319:                                                                                                  #  VERB PROCEED WITHOUT DATA, VERB RESEQUENCE,
018809,002320:                                                                                                  #  ANOTHER MONITOR, OR ANY NVSUB CALL THAT PASSES THE DSPLOCK (PROVIDED
018810,002321:                                                                                                  #  THAT THE OPERATOR HAS SOMEHOW ALLOWED THE ENDING OF A MONITOR WHICH
018811,002322:                                                                                                  #  HE HAS INITIATED THROUGH THE KEYBOARD).
018812,002323: 
018813,002324:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR ACTION IS SUSPENDED, BUT NOT ENDED, BY ANY KEYBOARD ACTION,
018814,002325:                                                                                                  #  EXCEPT ERROR LIGHT RESET. IT BEGINS AGAIN WHEN KEY RELEASE IS PERFORMED.
018815,002326:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR SAVES THE NOUN AND APPROPRIATE DISPLAY VERB IN MONSAVE. IT SAVES
018816,002327:                                                                                                  #  NOUNCADR IN MONSAVE1, IF NOUN = MACHINE CADR TO BE SPECIFIED. BIT 15 OF
018817,002328:                                                                                                  #  MONSAVE1 IS THE KILL MONITOR SIGNAL (KILLER BIT). BIT 14 OF MONSAVE1
018818,002329:                                                                                                  #  INDICATES THE CURRENT MONITOR WAS EXTERNALLY INITIATED (EXTERNAL
018819,002330:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR BIT). IT IS TURNED OFF BY RELDSP AND KILMONON.
018820,002331: 
018821,002332:                                                                                                  #  MONSAVE INDICATES IF MONITOR IS ON (+=ON, +0=OFF)
018822,002333:                                                                                                  #  IF MONSAVE IS +, MONITOR ENTERS NO REQUEST, BUT TURNS KILLER BIT OFF.
018823,002334:                                                                                                  #  IF MONSAVE IS +0, MONITOR ENTERS REQUEST AND TURNS KILLER BIT OFF.
018824,002335: 
018825,002336:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB (IF EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT IS OFF), VB=PROCEED WITHOUT DATA,
018826,002337:                                                                                                  #  VB=RESEQUENCE, AND VB=TERMINATE TURN KILL MONITOR BIT ON.
018827,002338: 
018828,002339:                                                                                                  #  IF KILLER BIT IS ON, MONREQ ENTERS NO FURTHER REQUESTS, ZEROS MONSAVE
018829,002340:                                                                                                  #  AND MONSAVE1 (TURNING OFF KILLER BIT AND EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT).
018830,002341: 
018831,002342:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR DOSENT TEST FOR MATBS SINCE NVSUB CAN HANDLE INTERNAL MATBS NOW
018832,002343:

018957,002468:                                                                                                  #  DSPFMEM IS USED TO DISPLAY (IN OCTAL) ANY FIXED REGISTER.
018958,002469:                                                                                                  #  IT IS USED WITH NOUN = MACHINE CADR TO BE SPECIFIED. THE FCADR OF THE 
018959,002470:                                                                                                  #  DESIRED LOCATION IS THEN PUNCHED IN. IT HANDLES F/F (FCADR 4000-7777)
018960,002471:                                                                                                  #  
018961,002472:                                                                                                  #  FOR BANKS L/E 27, THIS IS ENOUGH.
018962,002473: 
018963,002474:                                                                                                  #  FOR BANKS G/E 30, THE THIRD COMPONENT OF NOUN 26 (PRIO, ADRES, BBCON)
018964,002475:                                                                                                  #  MUST BE PRELOADED WITH THE DESIRED SUPERBANK BITS (BITS 5,6,7).
018965,002476:                                                                                                  #        V23N26 SHOULD BE USED.
018966,002477: 
018967,002478:                                                                                                  #  SUMMARY
018968,002479:                                                                                                  #  FOR BANKS L/E 27,                             V27N01E(FCADR)E
018969,002480:                                                                                                  #  FOR BANKS G/E 30,     V23N26E(SUPERBITS)E     V27N01E(FCADR)E
018970,002481: 
018971,002482: 41,3353           34317        DSPFMEM            CAF      R1D1                                  #  IF F/F, DATACALL USES BANK 02 OR 03.
018972,002483: 41,3354           54777                           TS       DSPCOUNT                              
018973,002484: 41,3355           31047                           CA       DSPTEM1    +2                         #  SUPERBANK BITS WERE PRELOADED INTO
018974,002485: 41,3356           54001                           TS       L                                     #  3RD COMPONENT OF NOUN 26.
018975,002486: 41,3357           31017                           CA       NOUNCADR                              #  ORIGINAL FCADR LOADED STILL IN NOUNCADR.
018976,002487: 41,3360           04651                           TC       SUPDACAL                              #  CALL WITH FCADR IN A, SUPERBITS IN L.
018977,002488: 41,3361           03363                           TC       DSPOCTWD                              
018978,002489: 41,3362           05155        ENDSPF             TC       ENDOFJOB                              
018979,002490:

Page 450 

019395,002906: 
019396,002907:                                                                                                  #  KEY RELEASE ROUTINE
019397,002908: 
019398,002909:                                                                                                  #  THIS ROUTINE ALWAYS TURNS OFF THE UPACT LIGHT AND ALWAYS CLEARS DSPLOCK.
019399,002910: 
019400,002911:                                                                                                  #  THE HIGHEST PRIORITY FUNCTION OF THE KEY RELEASE BUTTON IS THE
019401,002912:                                                                                                  #  UNSUSPENDING OF A SUSPENDED MONITOR WHICH WAS EXTERNALLY INITIATED.
019402,002913:                                                                                                  #  THIS FUNCTION IS ACCOMPLISHED BY CLEARING DSPLOCK AND TURNING OFF
019403,002914:                                                                                                  #  THE KEY RELEASE LIGHT IF BOTH DSPLIST AND CADRSTOR ARE EMPTY.
019404,002915: 
019405,002916:                                                                                                  #  IF NO SUCH MONITOR EXISTS, THEN RELDSP IS EXECUTED TO CLEAR DSPLOCK
019406,002917:                                                                                                  #  AND THE EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT (FREEING THE DISPLAY SYSTEM FOR INTERNAL
019407,002918:                                                                                                  #  USE), TURN OFF THE KEY RELEASE LIGHT, AND WAKE UP ANY JOB IN DSPLIST.
019408,002919: 
019409,002920:                                                                                                  #  IN ADDITION IF THERE IS A JOB IN ENDIDLE, THEN CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED
019410,002921:                                                                                                  #  TO PINBRNCH (IN DISPLAY INTERFACE ROUTINE) TO RE-EXECUTE THE SERIES OF
019411,002922:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB CALLS ETC. THAT PRECEDED THE ENDIDLE CALL STILL AWAITING RESPONSE.
019412,002923:                                                                                                  #  THIS FEATURE IS INTENDED FOR USE WHEN THE OPERATOR HAS BEEN REQUESTED TO
019413,002924:                                                                                                  #  RESPOND TO SOME INTERNAL ACTION THAT USED ENDIDLE, BUT HE HAS WRITTEN
019414,002925:                                                                                                  #  OVER THE INFORMATION ON THE DISPLAY PANEL BY SOME DISPLAYS OF HIS OWN
019415,002926:                                                                                                  #  INITIATION WHICH DO NOT SERVE AS RESPONSES. HITTING KEYRLSE WILL
019416,002927:                                                                                                  #  RE-ESTABLISH THE DISPLAYS TO THE STATE THEY WERE IN BEFORE HE OBSCURED
019417,002928:                                                                                                  #  THEM, SO THAT HE CAN SEE THE WAITING REQUEST. THIS WORKS ONLY FOR
019418,002929:                                                                                                  #  INTERNAL PROGRAMS THAT USED ENDIDLE THROUGH MARGARETS DISPLAY
019419,002930:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES.
019420,002931: 
019421,002932: 40,3461           44751        VBRELDSP           CS       BIT3                                  
019422,002933: 40,3462           00006                           EXTEND                                         
019423,002934: 40,3463           03011                           WAND     DSALMOUT                              #  TURN OFF UPACT LITE
019424,002935: 40,3464           10115                           CCS      21/22REG                              #  OLD DSPLOCK
019425,002936: 40,3465           34736                           CAF      BIT14                                 
019426,002937: 40,3466           71021                           MASK     MONSAVE1                              #  EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT (EMB)
019427,002938: 40,3467           10000                           CCS      A                                     
019428,002939: 40,3470           03477                           TC       UNSUSPEN                              #  OLD DSPLOCK AND EMB BOTH 1, UNSUSPEND.
019429,002940: 40,3471           04457        TSTLTS4            TC       RELDSP                                #  NOT UNSUSPENDING EXTERNAL MONITOR,
019430,002941: 40,3472           11042                           CCS      CADRSTOR                              #        RELEASE DISPLAY SYSTEM AND
019431,002942: 40,3473           03475                           TC       +2                                    #        DO RE-ESTABLISH IF CADRSTOR IS FULL.
019432,002943: 40,3474           05155                           TC       ENDOFJOB                              
019433,002944: 40,3475           04635                           TC       POSTJUMP                              
019434,002945: 40,3476           21050                           CADR     PINBRNCH                              
019435,002946: 40,3477           34755        UNSUSPEN           CAF      ZERO                                  #  EXTERNAL MONITOR IS SUSPENDED,
019436,002947: 40,3500           55012                           TS       DSPLOCK                               #        JUST UNSUSPEND IT BY CLEARING DSPLOCK.
019437,002948: 40,3501           11042                           CCS      CADRSTOR                              #        TURN KEY RELEASE LIGHT OFF IF BOTH
019438,002949: 40,3502           05155                           TC       ENDOFJOB                              #        CADRSTOR AND DSPLIST ARE EMPTY.
019439,002950: 40,3503           04502                           TC       RELDSP1                               
019440,002951: 40,3504           05155                           TC       ENDOFJOB                              
019441,002952: 
019442,002953: 40,3505                        ENDRELDS           EQUALS                                         
019443,002954:

Page 451 

019445,002956:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB IS USED FOR SUBROUTINE CALLS FROM WITHIN COMPUTER. IT CAN BE
019446,002957:                                                                                                  #  USED TO CALL THE COMBINATION OF ANY DISPLAY, LOAD, OR MONITOR VERB
019447,002958:                                                                                                  #  TOGETHER WITH ANY NOUN AVAILABLE TO THE KEYBOARD.
019448,002959:                                                                                                  #  PLACE 0VVVVVVVNNNNNNN INTO A.
019449,002960:                                                                                                  #  V-S ARE THE 7 BIT VERB CODE.  N-S ARE THE 7 BIT NOUN CODE.
019450,002961: 
019451,002962:                                                                                                  #  IF NVSUB IS CALLED WITH THE FOLLOWING NEGATIVE NUMBERS (RATHER THAN THE
019452,002963:                                                                                                  #  VERB-NOUN CODE) IN A, THEN THE DISPLAY IS BLANKED AS FOLLOWS -
019453,002964:                                                                                                  #   -4 FULL BLANK, -3 LEAVE MODE, -2 LEAVE MODE AND VERB, -1 BLANK R-S ONLY
019454,002965: 
019455,002966:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB CAN BE USED WITH MACH CADR TO BE SPEC BY PLACING THE CADR INTO
019456,002967:                                                                                                  #  MPAC+2 BEFORE THE STANDARD NVSUB CALL.
019457,002968: 
019458,002969:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB RETURNS TO 2+ CALLING LOC AFTER PERFORMING TASK, IF DISPLAY
019459,002970:                                                                                                  #  SYSTEM IS AVAILABLE. THE NEW NOUN AND VERB CODES ARE DISPLAYED.
019460,002971:                                                                                                  #  IF V:S =0, THE NEW NOUN CODE IS DISPLAYED ONLY (RETURN WITH NO FURTHER
019461,002972:                                                                                                  #  ACTION). IF N-S =0, THE NEW VERB CODE IS DISPLAYED ONLY (RETURN WITH NO
019462,002973:                                                                                                  #  FURTHER ACTION).
019463,002974: 
019464,002975:                                                                                                  #  IT RETURNS TO 1+ CALLING LOC WITHOUT PERFORMING TASK, IF DISPLAY
019465,002976:                                                                                                  #  SYSTEM IS BLOCKED (NOTHING IS DISPLAYED IN THIS CASE).
019466,002977:                                                                                                  #  IT DOES TC ABORT (WITH OCT 01501) IF IT ENCOUNTERS A DISPLAY PROGRAM
019467,002978:                                                                                                  #  ALARM CONDITION BEFORE RETURN TO CALLER.
019468,002979: 
019469,002980:                                                                                                  #  THE DISPLAY SYSTEM IS BLOCKED BY THE DEPRESSION OF ANY
019470,002981:                                                                                                  #  KEY, EXCEPT ERROR LIGHT RESET
019471,002982:                                                                                                  #  IT IS RELEASED BY THE KEY RELEASE BUTTON, ALL EXTENDED VERBS,
019472,002983:                                                                                                  #  PROCEED WITHOUT DATA, TERMINATE, RESEQUENCE, INITIALIZE EXECUTIVE,
019473,002984:                                                                                                  #  RECALL PART OF RECALTST IF ENDIDLE WAS USED,
019474,002985:                                                                                                  #  VB = REQUEST EXECUTIVE, VB = REQUEST WAITLIST,
019475,002986:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR SET UP.
019476,002987: 
019477,002988:                                                                                                  #  THE DISPLAY SYSTEM IS ALSO BLOCKED BY THE EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT, WHICH
019478,002989:                                                                                                  #  INDICATES AN EXTERNALLY INITIATED MONITOR IS RUNNING (SEE MONITOR)
019479,002990: 
019480,002991:                                                                                                  #  A NVSUB CALL THAT PASSES DSPLOCK AND THE EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT ENDS OLD
019481,002992:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR.
019482,002993: 
019483,002994:                                                                                                  #  DSPLOCK IS THE INTERLOCK FOR USE OF KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY SYSTEM WHICH
019484,002995:                                                                                                  #  LOCKS OUT INTERNAL USE WHENEVER THERE IS EXTERNAL KEYBOARD ACTION.
019485,002996: 
019486,002997:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB SHOULD BE USED TWICE IN SUCCESSION FOR :PLEASE PERFORM: SITUATIONS
019487,002998:                                                                                                  #  (SIMILARLY FOR PLEASE MARK).  FIRST PLACE THE CODED NUMBER FOR WHAT
019488,002999:                                                                                                  #  ACTION IS DESIRED OF OPERATOR INTO THE REGISTERS REFERRED TO BY THE
019489,003000:                                                                                                  #  :CHECKLIST: NOUN. GO TO NVSUB WITH A DISPLAY VERB AND THE :CHECKLIST:
019490,003001:                                                                                                  #  NOUN.  GO TO NVSUB AGAIN WITH THE :PLEASE PERFORM: VERB AND ZEROS IN THE
019491,003002:                                                                                                  #  LOW 7 BITS. THIS :PASTES UP: THE :PLEASE PERFORM: VERB INTO THE VERB
019492,003003:                                                                                                  #  LIGHTS.
019493,003004: 
019494,003005:                                                                                                  #  NVMONOPT IS AN ENTRY SIMILAR TO NVSUB, BUT REQUIRING AN ADDITIONAL

Page 452 

019496,003007:                                                                                                  #  PARAMETER IN L. IT SHOULD BE USED ONLY WITH A MONITOR VERB-NOUN CODE IN
019497,003008:                                                                                                  #  A. AFTER EACH MONITOR DISPLAY A *PLEASE* VERB WILL BE PASTED IN THE VERB
019498,003009:                                                                                                  #  LIGHTS OR DATA WILL BE BLANKED (OR BOTH) ACCORDING TO THE OPTIONS
019499,003010:                                                                                                  #  SPECIFIED IN L. IF BITS 8-14 OF L ARE OTHER THAN ZERO, THEN THEY WILL 
019500,003011:                                                                                                  #  BE INTERPRETED AS A VERB CODE AND PASTED IN THE VERB LIGHTS. (THIS VERB
019501,003012:                                                                                                  #  CODE SHOULD DESIGNATE ONE OF THE *PLEASE* VERBS.)  IF BITS 1-3 OF L ARE
019502,003013:                                                                                                  #  OTHER THAN ZERO, THEN THEY WILL BE USED TO BLANK DATA BY BEING FED TO
019503,003014:                                                                                                  #  BLANKSUB.  IF NVMONOPT IS USED WITH A VERB OTHER THAN A MONITOR VERB,
019504,003015:                                                                                                  #  THE PARAMETER IN L HAS NO EFFECT.
019505,003016: 
019506,003017:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB IN FIXED-FIXED PLACES 2+CALLING LOC INTO NVQTEM, TC NVSUBEND INTO
019507,003018:                                                                                                  #  ENTRET. (THIS WILL RESTORE OLD CALLING BANK BITS)
019508,003019:

019616,003127:                                                                                                  #  NOUNCADR IN ENTPAS0 (INTMCTBS).

019619,003130:    4204                                           COUNT*   $$/PIN                                
019620,003131:                                                                                                  #  FORCE BIT 15 OF MONSAVE1 TO 1.
019621,003132:    4204           34735        KILMONON           CAF      BIT15                                 #        THIS IS THE KILL MONITOR BIT.
019622,003133:    4205           55021                           TS       MONSAVE1                              #  TURN OFF BIT 14, THE EXTERNAL
019623,003134:                                                                                                  #        MONITOR BIT.
019624,003135:    4206           00002                           TC       Q                                     
019625,003136: 
019626,003137:                                                                                                  #  LOADSTAT      +0      INACTIVE (WAITING FOR DATA). SET BY NVSUB
019627,003138:                                                                                                  #                +1      PROCEED NO DATA. SET BY SPECIAL VERB
019628,003139:                                                                                                  #                -1      TERMINATE  SET BY SPECIAL VERB
019629,003140:                                                                                                  #                -0              DATA IN         SET BY END OF LOAD ROUTINE
019630,003141:                                                                                                  #                        OR      RESEQUENCE      SET BY VERB 32
019631,003142: 
019632,003143:                                                                                                  #  L TC ENDIDLE (FIXED FIXED)
019633,003144:                                                                                                  #  ROUTINES THAT REQUEST LOADS THROUGH NVSUB SHOULD USE ENDIDLE WHILE
019634,003145:                                                                                                  #  WAITING FOR THE DATA TO BE LOADED. ENDIDLE PUTS CURRENT JOB TO SLEEP.
019635,003146:                                                                                                  #  ENDIDLE CANNOT BE CALLED FROM ERASABLE OR F/F MEMORY,
019636,003147:                                                                                                  #  SINCE JOB SLEEP AND JOBWAKE CAN HANDLE ONLY FIXED BANKS.
019637,003148:                                                                                                  #  RECALTST TESTS LOADSTAT AND WAKES JOB UP TO,
019638,003149:                                                                                                  #        L+1     FOR TERMINATE
019639,003150:                                                                                                  #        L+2     FOR PROCEED WITHOUT DATA
019640,003151:                                                                                                  #        L+3     FOR DATA IN, OR RESEQUENCE
019641,003152:                                                                                                  #  IT DOES NOTHING IF LOADSTAT INDICATES WAITING FOR DATA.
019642,003153: 
019643,003154:                                                                                                  #  ENDIDLE ABORTS (WITH CODE 01206) IF A SECOND JOB ATTEMPTS TO GO TO SLEEP

Page 455 

019645,003156:                                                                                                  #  IN PINBALL. IN PARTICULAR, IF AN ATTEMPT IS MADE TO GO TO ENDIDLE WHEN
019646,003157:                                                                                                  #  1)    CADRSTOR NOT= +0. THIS IS THE CASE WHERE THE CAPACITY OF ENDIDLE IS
019647,003158:                                                                                                  #        EXCEEDED. (+-NZ INDICATE A JOB IS ALREADY ASLEEP DUE TO ENDIDLE.)
019648,003159:                                                                                                  #  2)    DSPLIST NOT= +0. THIS INDICATES A JOB IS ALREADY ASLEEP DUE TO
019649,003160:                                                                                                  #        NVSUBUSY.
019650,003161: 
019651,003162:    4207           22002        ENDIDLE            LXCH     Q                                     #  RETURN ADDRESS INTO L.
019652,003163:    4210           04220                           TC       ISCADR+0                              #  ABORT IF CADRSTOR NOT= +0
019653,003164:    4211           04224                           TC       ISLIST+0                              #  ABORT IF DSPLIST NOT= +0
019654,003165:    4212           30001                           CA       L                                     #  DONT SET DSPLOCK TO 1 SO CAN USE
019655,003166:    4213           75012                           MASK     LOW10                                 #  ENDIDLE WITH NVSUB INITIATED MONITOR.
019656,003167:    4214           60004                           AD       FBANK                                 #  SAME STRATEGY FOR CADR AS MAKECADR.
019657,003168:    4215           55042                           TS       CADRSTOR                              
019658,003169:    4216           05133                           TC       JOBSLEEP                              
019659,003170: 
019660,003171:    4217           05155        ENDINST            TC       ENDOFJOB                              
019661,003172: 
019662,003173:    4220           11042        ISCADR+0           CCS      CADRSTOR                              #  ABORTS (CODE 01206) IF CADRSTOR NOT= +0.
019663,003174:    4221           04227                           TC       DSPABORT                              #  RETURNS IF CADRSTOR = +0.
